It‚Äôs been a while, everyone.

As I was rearranging the contents for completion, various developments came to mind. The reason for this is that I couldn‚Äôt write them out easily, because which one to adopt would have a big impact on the future.

Oops, there‚Äôs still some revision work to be done before that.

Proofreading is really great. They don‚Äôt just look for inconsistencies in the current volume, they look for errors in the entire volume.

However, with so many volumes, it seems that small discrepancies can pile up. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶

It would be easier if it was just a typo or a rewrite to make the text easier to understand or something like that.

In my case, I started writing with only a rough plot, so I had to complete most of the checking only in my mind. I was reminded that I would only be able to do that for a short number of books, and that in the future I would try to boil down the plot before I started writing.

So, here we are with the nineteenth volume.

The last war has broken out, and forces are staring each other in the face in many places. I can‚Äôt write everything in this volume, and will continue in the next volume as a matter of course.

Here‚Äôs how I‚Äôm going to plow through the remaining three books (planned)!

It‚Äôs not uncommon for me to change my direction as I write. I will continue to devote myself to thinking up new stories so that readers can enjoy them more!
